data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="layout" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="flex xs12 row" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__text center" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><h2 data-v-5fa1a0d6>Reporting is Built in at Every Level</h2></div></div></div></div></div><div class="flex xs12 row" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div data-v-5fa1a0d6><div style="position:relative;left:25%" data-v-5fa1a0d6><table><tr><th style="font-size:2em;padding-right:15px">Student & Adult Users<td style="height:100px"><div style="height:90%;border-left:3px solid #4f8db3;padding:5.5px;bottom:undefinedpx"><p style="max-width:48%;padding-left:25px;font-size:1.5em">Students and adults can view reports that help them gauge their progress and connect their next steps to ultimate goals. They can also view a comprehensive cross-section of all assessments taken and which occupations show up multiple times.</div><tr><th style="font-size:2em;padding-right:15px">Site Administrators & Staff Accounts<td style="height:100px"><div style="height:90%;border-left:3px solid #4f8db3;padding:undefinedpx;bottom:undefinedpx"><p style="max-width:48%;padding-left:25px;font-size:1.5em">The Site Administrator for a school, office, or other organization has top-level administrative priviledges to report on all aspects of saved activities, components, and progress of users. Staff Accounts provide the next level below of controlled administrative access.</div><tr><th style="font-size:2em;padding-right:15px">District or Regional Administrators<td style="height:100px"><div style="height:90%;border-left:3px solid #4f8db3;padding:undefinedpx;bottom:undefinedpx"><p style="max-width:48%;padding-left:25px;font-size:1.5em">District or Regional Administrators can view aggregated reports from all sites under their jurisdiction, as well as slice & dice data across sites or drill down to specific sites and metrics.</div><tr><th style="font-size:2em;padding-right:15px">Statewide Operators<td style="height:100px"><div style="height:90%;border-left:3px solid #4f8db3;padding:undefinedpx;bottom:undefinedpx"><p style="max-width:48%;padding-left:25px;font-size:1.5em">Statewide Operators of the CIS Platform have full access to all reporting metrics across regions and sites. Development tools are provided for custom report generation as well as customization services.</div></table></div></div></div><div data-v-d3caac66 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="hidden-sm-and-down" style="width:100%" data-v-d3caac66><div class="layout float" data-v-d3caac66 data-v-d3caac66><div class="flex xl12" data-v-d3caac66 data-v-d3caac66><div class="borders" data-v-d3caac66><div class="parallax" style="height:750px;background-color:#fff" data-v-d3caac66><div class="parallax__image-container"><img src="/boylayingdown3.jpg" class="parallax__image" style="display:block;transform:translate3d(-50%,nullpx,0)"></div><div class="parallax__content"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="hidden-md-and-up" data-v-d3caac66><img src="/boylayingdown3.jpg" class="borders" style="width:100%;background-color:#fff" data-v-d3caac66></div></div><div class="max" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="flex xs12" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="center xlargeText" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Compound Knowledge Year over Year<div class="hidden-sm-and-down" data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6></div><div style="max-width:1050px;position:relative;left:10%" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="layout row-md column child-flex-md" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="flex xs4 sm6" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card ma-1 card--flat" style="height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><svg preserveAspectRatio="none" version="1.1" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" x="0px" y="0px" width="500px" height="500px" viewBox="0 0 364.711 393.5" enable-background="new 0 0 364.711 393.5" xml:space="preserve" class="hidden-md-and-down" style="position:relative;top:50px;right:25%" data-v-5fa1a0d6><g id="s-Image_26-blue_circle_x2C__ring"><path fill="#B0D2DF" d="M181.222,72.725c34.054,0,66.072,13.262,90.154,37.343c24.08,24.081,37.342,56.099,37.342,90.154

It involves numerous decisions about educational opportunities, work experiences, and economic realities. Portfolios in CIS provide students and adults with the tools to make informed decisions at key points in their lives.</p><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="smallText center" style="font-size:1.5em" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Portfolios in CIS are lifelong. Students build on their career plans every year in CIS and can continue to use their Portfolios after graduation. Portfolios are transferrable between schools, colleges, workforce centers, and all other sites.</p><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="smallText center" style="font-size:1.5em" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Students and adults return repeatedly to CIS because of the annually updated, high-quality labor market information and career exploration tools.</p><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="smallText center" style="font-size:1.5em" data-v-5fa1a0d6>When users save occupations, schools, scholarships, Career Plan reflections, and resumes to their Portfolios they are building a repository of knowledge that they can draw on for years to come.</div></div></div></div><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__text center" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><h2 data-v-5fa1a0d6>Customizable Product Offering</h2></div></div><div data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="hidden-md-and-down"><div class="container fluid"><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto"><div class="layout row-sm column child-flex-sm"><div class="flex xs2"><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto"><p class="headLocationAndSize"></div></div><div class="flex xs3"><div><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto"><div class="topdown"><img alt="" class="imageSize long" src="/careertrek.png" style="top:15px"></div></div></div></div><div class="flex xs6"><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto"><p class="largeText textLocation" style="position:relative;top:undefinedpx">Career Trek engages elementary-age students in highly interactive, developmentally-appropriate, and gamified career exploration. style="height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="layout row-md column child-flex-md" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card card--flat" achievement and career awareness. Sherlock integrates with CIS.</div><div class="card card--flat" style="padding-top:20px;padding-right:10px;height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__media" style="height:125px" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__media__background" style="background:url(/sherlockconnext.svg) center center/contain no-repeat"></div><div class="card__media__content"></div></div><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="center bigText" style="padding-right:50px;padding-top:15px" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Sherlock Connext is a college and higher education guidance survey that helps the orientation team and career center meet institutional goals of increasing retention and completion through effective career development interventions. Sherlock Connext integrates with CIS.</div><div class="card card--flat" style="padding-top:55px;height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__media" style="height:70px" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__media__background" style="background:url(/realitycheck.svg) center center/contain no-repeat"></div><div class="card__media__content"></div></div><p class="center bigText" style="padding-right:20px;padding-top:45px" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Reality Check teaches financial literacy by connecting career plans to lifestyle choices. This interactive tool includes regional cost-of-living data, enabling students and adults to compare the overall costs of their lifestyle preferences to the earning potential of their career plans. Reality Check is included in CIS, but can also be incorporated in custom financial literacy tools.</div></div></div></div><div class="layout row" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="flex" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6></div></div></div></div></div><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="max" data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="xlargeText center" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Seamless Integration<p class="mediumText center" data-v-5fa1a0d6>intoCareers constantly innovates to serve our partners. Integrations with 3rd party systems provide the next level of service, whether it's automatic account creation, digital credential and transcript transfer, or practice tests for high-stakes exams. We are always open to discussing how new integrations might serve the needs of your organization.<div data-v-d629dca4 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="hidden-md-and-down" data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><h4 class="center" style="font-weight:700" data-v-d629dca4>Single Sign-On and Account Rostering</h4><br data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><div class="max" data-v-d629dca4><div class="layout row wrap" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="flex xs4" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="card card--flat" style="position:relative;top:15px;right:10px;height:auto" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="card__media" style="height:80px" data-v-d629dca4><div class="card__media__background" style="background:url(/clever7.svg) center center/contain no-repeat"></div><div class="card__media__content"></div></div></div></div><div class="flex xs8" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><p class="largeText" style="border-left:3px solid #4f8db3;padding-left:20px" data-v-d629dca4>Clever is the preferred solution for single sign on and automated account administration. It provides schools and districts with a single-sign on integration between their existing Student Information System (SIS) and the CIS Platform at no extra cost. Automatic account rostering is also available.</div></div><br data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><div class="layout row wrap" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="flex xs4" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="card__media" style="height:70px;position:relative;bottom:10px;right:40px;top:30px" data-v-d629dca4><div class="card__media__background" style="background:url(/googlessobutton4.PNG) center center/contain no-repeat"></div><div class="card__media__content"></div></div></div></div><div class="flex xs8" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><p class="largeText" style="border-left:3px solid #4f8db3;padding-left:20px;position:relative;top:20px" data-v-d629dca4>Google for Education integrates directly with the CIS Platform, providing a single sign-on for students into their CIS Portfolios. Automatic account rostering is also available.</div></div><br data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><div class="layout row wrap" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="flex xs4" and districts with single-sign on integration with the CIS Platform.</div></div></div><br data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><h4 class="center" style="font-weight:700" class="center" data-v-5fa1a0d6><h1 class="smallH1">An Innovative Network of Peers</h1><br><p class="largeText">State operators of CIS systems from around the nation collaborate on a regular basis to exchange ideas and discuss career development innovations in their states. The CIS Network is comprised of leaders in their areas from across Secondary Education, Labor and Workforce, and Higher Education state offices.</p><br><p class="largeText">The CIS Network gathers yearly with intoCareers leadership to set research and development objectives, achieve common goals, and share creative strategies.</p><br><p class="largeText">In addition to exchanging ideas, state leaders collaborate more directly on projects to improve and develop new tools in the CIS Platform. These projects are often then able to be shared with other states as part of the base CIS Platform: a non-profit model which truly delivers year-over-year increased value and innovation at lower costs than private and for-profit vendor relationships.</p><br><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></div><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><div data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="hidden-md-and-down"><div class="layout row"><div class="flex xs4"><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto"><div><div><img alt="intoCareers" class="imgposition" src="/logo.png"></div></div></div></div><div class="flex xs8"><div class="card card--flat" style="height:100%"><div class="center" style="position:relative;top:35px"><h3 class="txtposition">An Experienced Partner</h3></div></div></div></div><br><br><br><p class="largeText center">intoCareers has collaborated with state agencies, non-profits, and institutions of higher education for over 45 years to deliver quality career development resources and tools that are consistently focused on individual outcomes. As a non-profit, we truly align with government and higher education values.</div><div class="hidden-md-and-up hidden-xs-only"><div><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto"><img Staff Accounts provide the next level below of controlled administrative access.</div><div class="max hidden-lg-and-up" data-v-024d0314><p class="center" style="font-size:2em;position:relative" data-v-024d0314>District or Regional Administrators<p style="font-size:1.15em" data-v-024d0314>District or Regional Administrators can view aggregated reports from all sites under their jurisdiction, as well as slice & dice data across sites or drill down to specific sites and metrics.</div><div class="max hidden-lg-and-up" data-v-024d0314><p class="center" style="font-size:2em;position:relative" data-v-024d0314>Statewide Operators<p style="font-size:1.15em" data-v-024d0314>Statewide Operators of the CIS Platform have full access to all reporting metrics across regions and sites. data-v-024d0314><div style="position:relative;top:undefinedpx;bottom:undefinedpx" data-v-024d0314><p style="font-size:1.05em" data-v-024d0314>Students and adults can view reports that help them gauge their progress and connect their next steps to ultimate goals. It involves numerous decisions about educational opportunities, work experiences, and economic realities. Portfolios in CIS provide students and adults with the tools to make informed decisions at key points in their lives.</p><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="smallText center" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Portfolios in CIS are lifelong. Students build on their career plans every year in CIS and can continue to use their Portfolios after graduation. Portfolios are transferrable between schools, colleges, workforce centers, and all other sites.</p><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="smallText center" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Students and adults return repeatedly to CIS because of the annually updated, high-quality labor market information and career exploration tools.</p><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="smallText center" data-v-5fa1a0d6>When users save occupations, schools, scholarships, Career Plan reflections, and resumes to their Portfolios they are building a repository of knowledge that they can draw on for years to come.</div></div></div></div><div data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><hr data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="mobileHeading center max" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Customizable Product Offering</p><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><div data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="hidden-md-and-down"><div class="container fluid"><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto"><div class="layout row-sm column child-flex-sm"><div class="flex xs2"><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto"><p class="headLocationAndSize"></div></div><div class="flex xs3"><div><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto"><div class="topdown"><img alt="" class="imageSize long" src="/careertrek.png" style="top:15px"></div></div></div></div><div class="flex xs6"><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto"><p class="largeText textLocation" style="position:relative;top:undefinedpx">Career Trek engages elementary-age students in highly interactive, developmentally-appropriate, and gamified career exploration. This interactive tool includes regional cost-of-living data, enabling students and adults to compare the overall costs of their lifestyle preferences to the earning potential of their career plans. Reality Check is included in CIS, but can also be incorporated in custom financial literacy tools.</div></div></div></div><div class="layout row" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="flex" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6></div></div></div></div></div><div class="hidden-md-and-up" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="max" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="layout row-md column child-flex-md" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card card--flat" style="padding-top:10px;height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__media" style="height:150px" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__media__background" style="background:url(/sherlock.png) center center/contain no-repeat"></div><div class="card__media__content"></div></div><p class="center bigText" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Sherlock is a secondary school guidance survey that enables counselors to effectively implement large and small-scale intervention programs by providing insight into individual student achievement and career awareness. Sherlock integrates with CIS.</div><div class="card card--flat" style="padding-top:20px;height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__media" style="height:85px" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__media__background" style="background:url(/connext.svg) center center/contain no-repeat"></div><div class="card__media__content"></div></div><p class="center bigText" style="padding-top:50px" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Sherlock Connext is a college and higher education guidance survey that helps the orientation team and career center meet institutional goals of increasing retention and completion through effective career development interventions. Sherlock Connext integrates with CIS.</div><div class="card card--flat" style="padding-top:40px;height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__media" style="height:70px" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__media__background" style="background:url(/realitycheck.svg) center center/contain no-repeat"></div><div class="card__media__content"></div></div><p class="center bigText" style="padding-top:45px" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Reality Check teaches financial literacy by connecting career plans to lifestyle choices. This interactive tool includes regional cost-of-living data, enabling students and adults to compare the overall costs of their lifestyle preferences to the earning potential of their career plans. Reality Check is included in CIS, but can also be incorporated in custom financial literacy tools.</div></div></div></div></div><br data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="max center hidden-lg-and-up" data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="mobileHeading" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Seamless Integration<p class="largeText" data-v-5fa1a0d6>intoCareers constantly innovates to serve our partners. Integrations with 3rd party systems provide the next level of service, whether it's automatic account creation, digital credential and transcript transfer, or practice tests for high-stakes exams. We are always open to discussing how new integrations might serve the needs of your organization.</div><div class="hidden-lg-and-up" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="hidden-md-and-down" data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><h4 class="center" style="font-weight:700" data-v-d629dca4>Single Sign-On and Account Rostering</h4><br data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><div class="max" data-v-d629dca4><div class="layout row wrap" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="flex xs4" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="card card--flat" style="position:relative;top:15px;right:10px;height:auto" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="card__media" style="height:80px" data-v-d629dca4><div class="card__media__background" style="background:url(/clever7.svg) center center/contain no-repeat"></div><div class="card__media__content"></div></div></div></div><div class="flex xs8" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><p class="largeText" style="border-left:3px solid #4f8db3;padding-left:20px" data-v-d629dca4>Clever is the preferred solution for single sign on and automated account administration. It provides schools and districts with a single-sign on integration between their existing Student Information System (SIS) and the CIS Platform at no extra cost. Automatic account rostering is also available.</div></div><br data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><div class="layout row wrap" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="flex xs4" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="card__media" style="height:70px;position:relative;bottom:10px;right:40px;top:30px" data-v-d629dca4><div class="card__media__background" style="background:url(/googlessobutton4.PNG) center center/contain no-repeat"></div><div class="card__media__content"></div></div></div></div><div class="flex xs8" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><p class="largeText" style="border-left:3px solid #4f8db3;padding-left:20px;position:relative;top:20px" data-v-d629dca4>Google for Education integrates directly with the CIS Platform, providing a single sign-on for students into their CIS Portfolios. Automatic account rostering is also available.</div></div><br data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><div class="layout row wrap" data-v-d629dca4 data-v-d629dca4><div class="flex xs4" and districts with single-sign on integration with the CIS Platform.</div></div></div><br data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><br data-v-d629dca4><h4 class="center" style="font-weight:700" class="center max hidden-lg-and-up" data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="center mobileHeading hidden-lg-and-up" data-v-5fa1a0d6>An Innovative Network of Peers<p class="center largeText hidden-lg-and-up" data-v-5fa1a0d6>State operators of CIS systems from around the nation collaborate on a regular basis to exchange ideas and discuss career development innovations in their states. The CIS Network is comprised of leaders in their areas from across Secondary Education, Labor and Workforce, and Higher Education state offices.<p class="center largeText hidden-lg-and-up" data-v-5fa1a0d6>The CIS Network gathers yearly with intoCareers leadership to set research and development objectives, achieve common goals, and share creative strategies.<p class="center largeText hidden-lg-and-up" data-v-5fa1a0d6>In addition to exchanging ideas, state leaders collaborate more directly on projects to improve and develop new tools in the CIS Platform. These projects are often then able to be shared with other states as part of the base CIS Platform: a non-profit model which truly delivers year-over-year increased value and innovation at lower costs than private and for-profit vendor relationships.</div><div class="hidden-md-and-down hidden-lg-and-up" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="layout row" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="flex xs4" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div data-v-5fa1a0d6><div data-v-5fa1a0d6><img alt="intoCareers" class="imgposition" src="/logo.png" data-v-5fa1a0d6></div></div></div></div><div class="flex xs8" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card card--flat" style="height:100%" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="center" style="position:relative;top:35px" data-v-5fa1a0d6><h3 class="txtposition" data-v-5fa1a0d6>An Experienced Partner</h3></div></div></div></div></div><div class="max" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div style="position:relative;top:50px" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="hidden-lg-and-up center mobileHeading" data-v-5fa1a0d6><p data-v-5fa1a0d6>An experienced partner</div><p class="center largeText hidden-lg-and-up" data-v-5fa1a0d6>intoCareers has collaborated with state agencies, non-profits, and institutions of higher education for over 45 years to deliver quality career development resources and tools that are consistently focused on individual outcomes. As a non-profit, we truly align with government and higher education values.</div><div class="hidden-lg-and-up" data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__text" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="largeText center" data-v-5fa1a0d6>1970s<p class="mediumText center" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Academic research launches innovated career development solution.</div></div><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__text" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="largeText center" data-v-5fa1a0d6>1980s & 1990s<p class="mediumText center" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Evolution of the CIS Platform driven by field-based research and experience.</div></div><div class="card card--flat" style="height:auto" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><div class="card__text" data-v-5fa1a0d6 data-v-5fa1a0d6><p class="largeText center" data-v-5fa1a0d6>2000 - Present<p class="mediumText center" data-v-5fa1a0d6>Flexible, comprehensive online platform.
